    function createJWScriptTag(scriptSrc, callback) {
            const s = document.createElement('script');
            s.id = 'JWPlayerLibrary'
            s.type = 'text/javascript';
            s.src = scriptSrc;
            s.onload = callback;
            document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(s);
    }

    function detectDeviceAndLoadJWScript(callback) {
            if(navigator.userAgent.match(/Android/i) || navigator.userAgent.match(/webOS/i) || navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone/i) || navigator.userAgent.match(/iPad/i) || navigator.userAgent.match(/iPod/i) || navigator.userAgent.match(/BlackBerry/i) || navigator.userAgent.match(/Windows Phone/i)) {
                createJWScriptTag("https://cdn.jwplayer.com/libraries/01cQTbgr.js", callback);
            } else {
                createJWScriptTag("https://cdn.jwplayer.com/libraries/iijH6IUf.js", callback);
            }
    }

                The billionaire chairman and co-founder of Dish Network&#039;s compensation was up sharply from $2.35 million in 2019 owing to option awards.

        let device;
        var mobile = /(?:phone|windows\s+phone|ipod|blackberry|(?:android|bb\d+|meego|silk|googlebot) .+?mobile|palm|windows\s+ce|opera mini|avantgo|docomo)/i;
        var tablet = /(?:ipad|playbook|(?:android|bb\d+|meego|silk)(?! .+? mobile))/i;
        if(mobile.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
            device = "mobile";
        } else if(tablet.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
            device = "tablet";
        } else {
            device = "desktop";
        }
        return device;
    };       
    let overideAdZoneIfApplicable = function(adZone) {
        let curPathName = window.location.pathname;
        const constants = {
            chartPageAdUnits: {
                hot100: 'charts/hot-100',
                billboard200: 'charts/billboard-200',
                rbhiphopsongs: 'charts/r-b-hip-hop-albums',
                hot100songs: 'charts/year-end/Hot-100'
            }
        };
        if( curPathName == '/charts/hot-100' ||
            curPathName == '/charts/billboard-200' ||
            curPathName == '/charts/r-b-hip-hop-songs' ||
            curPathName == '/charts/year-end/2018/hot-100-songs' ) {
            const splitPathName = curPathName.split('/');
            let chartLastPath = splitPathName[splitPathName.length-1];
            chartLastPath = chartLastPath.split('-');
            chartLastPath = chartLastPath.join('');
            adZone = constants.chartPageAdUnits[chartLastPath];
        }
        return adZone;
    };             
    var AdSlots = {};
    var blogherads = blogherads || {};
    blogherads.adq = blogherads.adq || [];
    if (window.top.pageLevelKeys !== null) {
        blogherads.adq.push(function() {
            for (const key in window.top.pageLevelKeys) {
                blogherads.setTargeting(key, window.top.pageLevelKeys[key]);
            }
        });
    }
    if (window.top.pageAdZoneFragment !== undefined && window.top.pageAdZoneFragment['zone'] !== null) {
        if (window.top.pageAdZoneFragment['zone'] === '' && window.top.pageLevelKeys !== undefined && window.top.pageLevelKeys['pt'] !== null && window.top.pageLevelKeys['pt'] !== '') {
            window.top.pageAdZoneFragment['zone'] = window.top.pageLevelKeys['pt'];
        }
        blogherads.adq.push(function() {
            let siteHostname = document.location.hostname;
            if (siteHostname.includes("billboard") || siteHostname.includes("hollywoodreporter")) {
                blogherads.setConf('vertical', `${overideAdZoneIfApplicable(window.top.pageAdZoneFragment['zone'])}`);
            } else if (siteHostname.includes("vibe")) {
                blogherads.setConf('vertical', `${detectDevice()}/${overideAdZoneIfApplicable(window.top.pageAdZoneFragment['zone'])}`);
            }
        });
    }
    var idMap = new Map();
    var pageAdsObserver = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
        var adElements = document.querySelectorAll('[data-dark-matter-is-processed="false"]');
        if (adElements.length != 0) {
            blogherads.adq.push(function() {
                for (let i = 0; i < adElements.length; i++) {
                    if (adElements[i].getAttribute("data-dark-matter-is-processed") !== "true") {
                        let adElementType = adElements[i].getAttribute("data-position");
                        adElementType = adElementType.trim().toLowerCase();
                        if (!idMap.has(adElementType)) {
                            idMap.set(adElementType, 1);
                        } else {
                            idMap.set(adElementType, idMap.get(adElementType) + 1);
                        }            
                        let adElementAttribute = document.createAttribute("id");
                        adElementAttribute.value = adElementType + "_" + idMap.get(adElementType);
                        adElements[i].setAttributeNode(adElementAttribute);  
                        if (adElementType === 'footerboard_ad') {
                            blogherads.defineResponsiveSlot([
                                [[728, 0], 'banner'],
                                [[0, 0], 'none']
                            ], adElementAttribute.value).addSize('banner', [970, 90]).setTargeting('pos', 'footerboard_ad').display();
                        } else if (adElementType === 'leaderboard_ad') {
                            blogherads.defineResponsiveSlot([
                                [[1024, 0], 'flexbanner'],
                                [[728, 0], 'banner'],
                                [[320, 0], 'tinybanner'],
                                [[0, 0], 'none']
                            ], adElementAttribute.value).addSize('tinybanner', [[320, 170], [320, 100]]).setTargeting('pos', 'leaderboard_ad').display();
                        } else if (adElementType === 'rightrail_ad') {
                            blogherads.defineResponsiveSlot([
                                [[1024, 0], 'flexrec'],
                                [[0, 0], 'none']
                            ], adElementAttribute.value).setTargeting('pos', 'rightrail_ad').display();				
                        } else if (adElementType === 'leftrail_ad') {
                            blogherads.defineResponsiveSlot([
                                [[1024, 600], 'flexrec'],
                                [[728, 250], 'medrec'],
                                [[320, 50], 'mobileincontent'],
                                [[0, 0], 'none']
                            ], adElementAttribute.value).setTargeting('pos', 'leftrail_ad').display();
                        } else if (adElementType === 'contentwell_ad') {
                            blogherads.defineResponsiveSlot([
                                [[320, 0], 'medrec'],
                                [[0, 0], 'none']
                            ], adElementAttribute.value).setTargeting('pos', 'contentwell_ad').display();
                        } else if (adElementType === 'parallax_ad') {
                            blogherads.defineResponsiveSlot([
                                [[1024, 0], 'none'],
                                [[320, 0], '300x600'],
                                [[0, 0], 'none']
                            ], adElementAttribute.value).setTargeting('pos', 'parallax_ad').display();
                        } else if (adElementType === 'native_ad') {
                            blogherads.defineResponsiveSlot([
                                [[1024, 250], 'flexbanner']
                                [[728, 90], 'banner'],
                                [[320, 480], 'tinybanner'],
                                [[0, 0], 'none']
                            ], adElementAttribute.value).setTargeting('pos', 'native_ad')
                            .addSize('tinybanner', [[2, 2], [4, 4], [320, 480]])
                            .addSize('banner', [[2, 2], [4, 4]])
                            .addSize('flexbanner', [[2, 2], [4, 4]]).display();
                        } else if (adElementType === 'adhesion') {
                            blogherads.defineSlot('bottom', 'skm-ad-bottom').setTargeting('pos', 'adhesion').display();
                        } else if (adElementType === 'promo') {
                            blogherads.defineCustomSlot(adElementAttribute.value, [[2, 2], [3, 3]]).setTargeting('pos', 'promo').display();
                        } else if (adElementType === 'zergnet') {
                            blogherads.defineCustomSlot(adElementAttribute.value, [4, 4]).setTargeting('pos', 'zergnet').setSubAdUnitPath('zergnet').setDefaultAutoRefreshTime(0).display();
                        } else if (adElementType === 'out_of_page') {
                            blogherads.defineSlot('inlineoop', adElementAttribute.value).setTargeting('pos', 'out_of_page').display();
                        } else if (adElementType === 'richmedia_ad') {
                            blogherads.defineCustomSlot(adElementAttribute.value, [1, 1]).setTargeting('pos', 'richmedia_ad').display();
                        } else if (adElementType === 'autoinject_ad') {
                            blogherads.defineResponsiveSlot([
                                [[728, 0], 'none'],
                                [[320, 0], 'mobileincontent'],
                                [[0, 0], 'none']
                            ], adElementAttribute.value).setTargeting('pos', 'autoinject_ad').display();
                        } else if (adElementType === 'middleboard_ad') {
                            blogherads.defineResponsiveSlot([
                                [[1024, 0], 'flexbanner'],
                                [[728, 0], 'banner'],
                                [[320, 0], 'mobileincontent'],
                                [[0, 0], 'none']
                            ], adElementAttribute.value).setTargeting('pos', 'middleboard_ad').display();
                        } else if (adElementType === 'fluidrail_ad') {
                            blogherads.defineResponsiveSlot([
                                [[1024, 600], 'flexrec'],
                                [[320, 50], 'medrec'],
                                [[0, 0], 'none']
                            ], adElementAttribute.value).setTargeting('pos', 'fluidrail_ad').display();
                        } else if (adElementType === 'interchart_ad') {
                            blogherads.defineResponsiveSlot([
                                [[1024, 0], 'flexbanner'],
                                [[728, 0], 'banner'],
                                [[320, 0], 'medrec'],
                                [[0, 0], 'none']
                            ], adElementAttribute.value).setTargeting('pos', 'interchart_ad').addSize('banner', [300, 250]).display();
                        } else if (adElementType === 'presentedby_ad') {
                            blogherads.defineCustomSlot(adElementAttribute.value, [[88, 31], [120, 60]]).setTargeting('pos', 'presentedby_ad').display();
                        } else if (adElementType === 'sponsor') {
                            blogherads.defineCustomSlot(adElementAttribute.value, [2, 3]).setTargeting('pos', 'sponsor').setDefaultAutoRefreshTime(0).display();
                        } else if (adElementType === '728x90_ad') {
                            blogherads.defineResponsiveSlot([
                                [[728, 0], 'banner'],
                                [[0, 0], 'none']
                            ], adElementAttribute.value).setTargeting('pos', '728x90_ad').display();
                        } else if (adElementType === 'chartrail_ad') {
                            blogherads.defineResponsiveSlot([
                                [[1024, 0], 'flexrec'],
                                [[728, 0], 'banner'],
                                [[320, 0], 'medrec'],
                                [[0, 0], 'none']
                            ], adElementAttribute.value).setTargeting('pos', 'chartrail_ad').addSize('banner', [300, 250]).display();
                        }
                        adElements[i].setAttribute("data-dark-matter-is-processed", "true");
                    }
                }
            });
        }
    });
    pageAdsObserver.observe(document, {attributes: false, childList: true, characterData: false, subtree:true});
  </script>
  <script ccpa-opt-out-geo="ca" ccpa-opt-out-ids="C0002,C0004,SPD_BG" ccpa-opt-out-lspa="true" charset="UTF-8" src="https://cdn.cookielaw.org/opt-out/otCCPAiab.js" type="text/javascript">
  </script>
  <script>
   function loadEUScript(source, attributes = {}) {

        const script = document.createElement('script');
        script.type = 'text/javascript';
        script.async = true;
        script.src = source;

        if (typeof attributes === 'object') {
            Object.keys(attributes).forEach(key => {
                script[key] = attributes[key];
                // check for data attribute.
                if (key.startsWith('data')) {
                    script.setAttribute(key, attributes[key]);
                }
            });
        } else if (typeof attributes === 'function') {
            attributes(script);
        }

        document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(script);
    }

    window.geofeed = function geofeed(options) {

        if (options === undefined || options === null || options.state === undefined || options.continent === undefined || options.state === null || options.continent === null) return;

        const state = options.state.toString();
        const continent = options.continent.toString();
        const cprLink = document.getElementById("california_privacy_rights_link");
        const cprLinkBlock = document.getElementById("california_privacy_rights_link_block");
        const dnsmpiLink = document.getElementById("do_not_sell_my_personal_information_link");
        const dnsmpiLinkBlock = document.getElementById("do_not_sell_my_personal_information_link_block");
        const eppLink = document.getElementById("eu_privacy_preferences_link");
        const eppLinkBlock = document.getElementById("eu_privacy_preferences_link_block");

        if (state !== 'CA' && state !== 'NY' && continent !== 'EU') {
            if (cprLinkBlock && cprLink && dnsmpiLinkBlock && dnsmpiLink && eppLinkBlock && eppLink) {
                cprLink.style.display = 'none'
                cprLinkBlock.style.display = 'none';
                dnsmpiLink.style.display = 'none';
                dnsmpiLinkBlock.style.display = 'none';
                eppLink.style.display = 'none';
                eppLinkBlock.style.display = 'none';
            }
        } else if (state === 'CA' || state === 'NY') {
            if (cprLinkBlock && cprLink && dnsmpiLinkBlock && dnsmpiLink && eppLinkBlock && eppLink) {
                cprLink.style.display = 'inline'
                cprLinkBlock.style.display = 'inline';
                dnsmpiLink.style.display = 'inline';
                dnsmpiLinkBlock.style.display = 'inline';
                eppLink.style.display = 'none';
                eppLinkBlock.style.display = 'none';

                dnsmpiLink.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    OneTrust.ToggleInfoDisplay();
                });                
            }
        } else if (continent === 'EU') {
            if (cprLinkBlock && cprLink && dnsmpiLinkBlock && dnsmpiLink && eppLinkBlock && eppLink) {
                cprLink.style.display = 'none'
                cprLinkBlock.style.display = 'none';
                dnsmpiLink.style.display = 'none';
                dnsmpiLinkBlock.style.display = 'none';
                eppLink.style.display = 'inline';
                eppLinkBlock.style.display = 'inline';
                loadEUScript("https://cdn.cookielaw.org/consent/tcf.stub.js", {
                    charset: "UTF-8",
                });
                eppLink.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    OneTrust.ToggleInfoDisplay();
                });
            }
        }
    }
  </script>

  </script>
